USA_the_desk_of_the_president = {

	USA_Hart_Bill_Countdown = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_document_building
		visible = {
		}
		available = { #Mission is completed when the player brings the bill to a vote
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = USA_bill_timer_pass_criteria

				always = no
			}
		}
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = bill_enable_mission_hart
		}
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = USA_bill_mission_deadline_hart

			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_hart_bill_timer_countdown_tt

						has_country_flag = USA_ted_kennedy_healthcare_bill

					check_if_bill_passed = yes

						limit = {
							has_country_flag = bill_passed
						}
						country_event = {
							id = hart.kennedy.5
							days = 1
						}
					}
					else = {
						country_event = {
							id = hart.kennedy.4
							days = 1
						}
					}
					clr_country_flag = bill_passed
					clr_country_flag = USA_ted_kennedy_healthcare_bill
					clr_country_flag = USA_chain_bill
					USA_bill_clear = yes
				}

	USA_chop_and_pray = {
		icon = GFX_decision_USA_rdc_r
		available = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { NPP_FR_senators = NPP_FR_supporting_senators }
					check_variable = { RD_R_senators = RD_R_supporting_senators }
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 50
		days_re_enable = 7
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_hart_presidency
			has_country_flag = bill_enable_mission_hart
		}
		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_rep_support_exchange_tt
			# recalculate
			set_temp_variable = { additional_pro_votes = NPP_C_senators }
			multiply_temp_variable = { additional_pro_votes = 0.3 }
			subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_supporting_senators = additional_pro_votes }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_C_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_C_senators
			}

			set_temp_variable = { additional_nat_votes = NPP_FR_senators }
			multiply_temp_variable = { additional_nat_votes = 0.2 }
			add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_supporting_senators = additional_nat_votes }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = NPP_FR_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = NPP_FR_senators
			}

			set_temp_variable = { additional_rep_votes = RD_R_senators }
			multiply_temp_variable = { additional_rep_votes = 0.2 }
			add_to_variable = { RD_R_supporting_senators = additional_rep_votes }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = RD_R_supporting_senators
				min = 0
				max = RD_R_senators
			}

			USA_initialize_bill_support_hart_dec = yes
			set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_management_efficiency_var = -0.04 }
			USA_management_efficiency_adjust = yes
			set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_equality_var = -0.04 }
			USA_equality_adjust = yes
			set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_var_civilrights_num = -0.04 }
			USA_civil_rights_relations_adjust = yes
		}
	}

	## BANKRUPCTCY CRISIS

	USA_HART_BANKRUPTCY_CRISIS_CAT = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_money
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_bankruptcy_response
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_hart_presidency
			has_country_flag = USA_bankruptcy_prevention_flag
		}
		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_toggle_visibility_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_crisis_visible_bankruptcy
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_crisis_visible_bankruptcy
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = USA_crisis_visible_bankruptcy
			}
		}
	}

	USA_emergency_budget_stimulus = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_economy_graph
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_bankruptcy_response
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_hart_presidency
			has_country_flag = USA_bankruptcy_prevention_flag
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_crisis_visible_bankruptcy }
		}
		days_remove = 14
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_bankruptcy_response
			## BAD THING HERE

			add_to_variable = { USA_bankruptcy_Response_var = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_var_budgethawk_num = 0.12 }
			USA_budget_hawk_adjust = yes
			set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_upkeep_cost_var = -0.09 }
			USA_upkeep_cost_adjust = yes
			set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_spending_power_var = -0.11 }
			USA_spending_power_adjust = yes
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_emergency_budget_stimulus"
			clr_country_flag = USA_bankruptcy_response
		}
	}

	USA_Zsa_Zsas_Game = {
		allowed = {
			always = no
			tag = USA
		}
		available = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_URI_Zsa_Zsa_running_amuck }
				has_country_flag = USA_Zsa_Zsa_Moved_On
			}
		}
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_diamond
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 7

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_citygoers
				}
				clr_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_citygoers
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_rural
				}
				clr_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_rural
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_civil_rights
				}
				clr_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_civil_rights
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_unions
				}
				clr_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_unions
			}
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					set_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_rural
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_zsa_zsa_delays_rural
				}
				25 = {
					set_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_citygoers
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_zsa_zsa_delays_citygoers
				}
				25 = {
					set_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_civil_rights
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_zsa_zsa_delays_civil_rights
				}
				25 = {
					set_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_unions
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_zsa_zsa_delays_unions
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { USA_zsa_zsa_contempt = 0.12 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = USA_zsa_zsa_contempt
				min = 0
				max = 1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { USA_zsa_zsa_contempt = 1 }
					}
					country_event = {
						id = chep.zsazsa.4
						days = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					activate_mission = USA_Zsa_Zsas_Game
				}
			}
		}
	}

	USA_URI_organization = {

			###### City Goers
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var_USA_URI_Leader_City_Goers = 1 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_citygoers }

				clamp_variable = {
					var = USA_URI_CityGoer_URI_Rep_Opp

					max = 0.99 # Chep can't completely organize anyone
				}
			}

					check_variable = { var_USA_URI_Leader_City_Goers = 2 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_citygoers }
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = USA_URI_CityGoer_URI_Rep_Opp
					value = USA_back_burner_boost
				}
				add_to_variable = { USA_URI_CityGoer_URI_Rep_Opp = 0.08 }
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = USA_URI_CityGoer_URI_Rep_Opp
				min = 0
				max = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_URI_CityGoer_URI_Rep_Opp = 1 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_citygoers_organized }
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_citygoers_organized
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { var_USA_URI_Leader_City_Goers = 2 }
						}
						# country_event = { # Jacobs doesn't have her own event
						#	id =
						#	days =
						# }
						USA_decrease_URI_coalition_strength = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#######

			###### Rural Folks
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var_USA_URI_Leader_Rural_Folk = 1 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_zsa_zsa_stalls_rural }
				}
				add_to_variable = { USA_URI_RuralFolk_URI_Rep_Opp = US_chep_scoring }
				clamp_variable = {

	USA_city_quota = {
		allowed = {
			always = no
			tag = USA
		}
		available = {
			has_country_flag = USA_chep_presidency
		}
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation

			factor = 100
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_Hart_meet_yearly_goals_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							var = USA_CITY_crime_rate
							value = USA_HART_Crime_Goal
							compare = greater_than
						}
						check_variable = {
							var = USA_CITY_homelessness
							value = USA_HART_Homelessness_Goal
							compare = greater_than
						}
						check_variable = {
							var = USA_CITY_poverty_rate
							value = USA_HART_Poverty_Goal
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_on_course_to_meet_goals_tt
				USA_HART_increase_senate_relations = yes
				USA_HART_increase_dem_stockpile_support = yes
				USA_HART_increase_rep_stockpile_support = yes
				set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_happiness_var = 0.09 }
				USA_happiness_adjust = yes
				set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_var_nimby_num = -0.08 }
				USA_NIMBY_relation_adjust = yes

				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_Hart_City_Goals_2 # meaning its cycle 3+
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = {
							id = hart.tree.31
							days = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							var = USA_CITY_crime_rate
							value = USA_HART_Crime_Goal
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
						check_variable = {
							var = USA_CITY_homelessness
							value = USA_HART_Homelessness_Goal
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
						check_variable = {
							var = USA_CITY_poverty_rate
							value = USA_HART_Poverty_Goal
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_not_on_course_to_meet_goals_tt
				USA_HART_decrease_senate_relations = yes
				USA_HART_decrease_dem_stockpile_support = yes
				USA_HART_decrease_rep_stockpile_support = yes
				set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_happiness_var = -0.03 }
				USA_happiness_adjust = yes
				set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_var_nimby_num = 0.03 }
				USA_NIMBY_relation_adjust = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = USA_Hart_City_Goals_1
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = USA_Hart_City_Goals_1
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = USA_Hart_City_Goals_2
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = USA_Hart_City_Goals_2

					}

						days = 1
					}
				}
			}

		}

	USA_topple_the_planters_empire = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_industrial_farm
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_active_police_activity
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_hart_presidency
			has_country_flag = USA_topple_the_planters_empire
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_srug_raid_success
					value = 0.06
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
		days_remove = 7
		days_re_enable = 45
		custom_cost_trigger = { always = yes } #no cost
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_Congress_Votes"
			set_country_flag = USA_active_police_activity
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = USA_active_police_activity
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_drug_bust_chances_tt
			set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_var_police_influence_num = 0.08 }
			USA_combatitive_crime_adjust = yes

			hidden_effect = {
				randomize_temp_variable = {
					var = USA_bust_successs
					distribution = uniform
					min = 0
					max = 1
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = USA_bust_successs
							value = USA_srug_raid_success
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
					# success
					set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_crime_rate_var = -0.06 }
					USA_crime_rate_adjust = yes
					set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_happiness_var = 0.03 }
					USA_happiness_adjust = yes
					set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_var_police_influence_num = -0.05 }
					USA_combatitive_crime_adjust = yes
					set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_var_nimby_num = -0.05 }
					USA_NIMBY_relation_adjust = yes
					add_to_variable = { USA_srug_raid_success = .06 }
				}
				else = {
					# epic fail
					set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_crime_rate_var = 0.03 }
					USA_crime_rate_adjust = yes
					set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_equality_var = -0.03 }
					USA_equality_adjust = yes
					set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_var_police_influence_num = 0.02 }
					USA_combatitive_crime_adjust = yes
					set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_var_budgethawk_num = 0.05 }
					USA_budget_hawk_adjust = yes
					set_temp_variable = { USA_temp_var_civilrights_num = -0.05 }
					USA_civil_rights_relations_adjust = yes
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { USA_srug_raid_success = -.12 }
		}
	}
}

			}

		}
	}

	USA_ongoing_leadership_play_p_mission = {
		icon = GFX_decision_USA_npp_p

		allowed = {
			always = no
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 90
		is_good = no # will pass if available met, will fail if time out
		selectable_mission = yes

		fire_only_once = no

		available = { # conditions for success
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = NPP_p_leadership_play_approval
				check_variable = { NPP_P_Leadership_Approval < 0.22 }
			}
		}

		complete_effect = { # play succeeds
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision complete USA_ongoing_leadership_play_p_mission"
			effect_tooltip = {
				USA_leadership_play_p_success_effect = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = USA.NPP_leadership.5 }
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = { # play fails
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision timeout USA_ongoing_leadership_play_p_mission"
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { NPP_N_Leadership_Approval < 0.22 } }
				effect_tooltip = {
					USA_leadership_play_n_success_effect = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = { id = USA.NPP_leadership.5 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { NPP_P_Leadership_Approval < 0.36 } }
				random_list = {
					1 = {
						effect_tooltip = {
							USA_leadership_play_p_fail_effect = yes
						}
						hidden_effect = {
							country_event = { id = USA.NPP_leadership.9 }
						}
					}
					1 = {
						effect_tooltip = {
							USA_leadership_play_p_success_effect = yes
						}
						hidden_effect = {
							country_event = { id = USA.NPP_leadership.5 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					USA_leadership_play_p_fail_effect = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = { id = USA.NPP_leadership.9 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# generic damage leadership
	USA_NPP_point_the_finger_for_caucus_failures = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_point
		available = {
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_active_NPP_leadership_play
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_AI_activated_NPP_leadership_play }
		}

		cost = 75
		days_re_enable = 30
		fire_only_once = no

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_NPP_point_the_finger_for_caucus_failures"
			set_temp_variable = { tempApproval = -0.1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = USA_ongoing_leadership_play_p_mission }
				USA_change_NPP_p_leadership_approval = yes

USA_politics_elections_category = {
	USA_view_results = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_voting
		allowed = {
			always = no
		}

		available = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = USA_senate_conclusion
				has_country_flag = USA_presidential_conclusion
			}
		}
	}
	USA_campaign_in_new_england = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_propaganda

		allowed = {
			tag = USA
		}

		available = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = currently_campaigning }
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 949
			}
		}

		#on_map_mode = map_only

		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 20

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_presidential_elections
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = USA_senate_conclusion
					has_country_flag = USA_presidential_conclusion
				}
			}
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_player_campaign_in_New_England
			set_country_flag = currently_campaigning

			set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_US_Election }
			remove_TNO_alert = yes
		}

		remove_effect = {
			USA_campaigning_effect = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}

	USA_campaign_in_east_coast = {

USA_draft_mobilization_category = {
	USA_no_war_demobilize = {
		allowed = { tag = USA }
		available = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = tno_conscription_volunteer_only
				has_idea = tno_conscription_disarmed_nation
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_mobilized_national_guard }
		}
		activation = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { USA_policing_variable > 0 }
					check_variable = { USA_advisor_variable > 0 }
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_idea = tno_conscription_limited_conscription
				has_idea = tno_conscription_broadened_conscription
				has_idea = tno_conscription_extensive_conscription
				has_country_flag = USA_mobilized_national_guard
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 90
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout USA_no_war_demobilize"
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_war_support = -0.10
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = tno_conscription_limited_conscription }
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = tno_conscription_volunteer_only
					remove_idea = tno_conscription_limited_conscription
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = tno_conscription_broadened_conscription }
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = tno_conscription_volunteer_only
					remove_idea = tno_conscription_broadened_conscription
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = tno_conscription_extensive_conscription }
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = tno_conscription_volunteer_only
					remove_idea = tno_conscription_extensive_conscription
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_mobilized_national_guard }
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "National Guard Infantry Division"
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "National Guard Armored Division"
				}
				hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = USA_mobilized_national_guard }
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_no_war_demobilize"
			#Your country doesn't explode, or something
		}

##################################################################

######### Response Tree mission

##################################################################

USA_react_to_last_potus = {
	respond_to_potus = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_clock
		available = { #Mission is completed when the player finishes their response tree
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = USA_response_mission_requirement_tt
				has_country_flag = USA_finished_response
			}
		}
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = USA_begin_response
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 180 #Undo the misstakes of the previous POTUS in 6 months or get screwed
		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = response_mission_fracture_party_tt
			add_stability = -0.07
			if = { #Check for what party is in charge and give their unity a severe blow
				limit = { #NPP
					OR = {
						has_government = progressivism
						has_government = paternalism
						has_government = national_socialism
						has_government = communist
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { USA_NPP_Unity = 5 }
			}
			else = { #RD
				subtract_from_variable = { USA_RD_Unity = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RDC_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_THURMOND_FR_NPP_Past
					}
				}
				USA_response_anger_north = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_response_anger_north_tt
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RDC_Past
					}
				}
				USA_response_anger_south = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_response_anger_south_tt
			}
		}
		complete_effect = { #Hooray you prevented the party from fracturing
			clr_country_flag = USA_begin_response
			hidden_effect = {
				USA_reload_presidential_tree = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

USA_MCS_Party_Unity_category = {

	mcs_talk_to_leaders_center = {
		icon = GFX_decision_USA_npp_p
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP
		}
		cost = 10
		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = MCS_talk_to_center
			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_variable = { mcs_change_influence_center = 0.01 }
				subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_right = 0.005 }
				subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_south = 0.01 }
				set_variable = { mcs_center_satisfaction_change = 0.1 }
				set_variable = { mcs_right_satisfaction_change = -0.05 }
				set_variable = { mcs_south_satisfaction_change = -0.1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { mcs_left_influence > 0.1 }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_left = 0.01 }
					set_variable = { mcs_left_satisfaction_change = 0.1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { mcs_fascist_influence > 0.1 }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_fascist = 0.01 }
					set_variable = { mcs_fascist_satisfaction_change = -0.1 }
				}
				mcs_influence_calculation = yes
				mcs_unity_check = yes
			}
		}
	}
	mcs_talk_to_leaders_right = {
		icon = GFX_decision_USA_npp
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP
		}
		cost = 10
		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = MCS_talk_to_business
			hidden_effect = {
				subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_center = 0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { mcs_change_influence_right = 0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { mcs_change_influence_south = 0.005 }
				set_variable = { mcs_center_satisfaction_change = -0.1 }
				set_variable = { mcs_right_satisfaction_change = 0.05 }
				set_variable = { mcs_south_satisfaction_change = 0.05 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { mcs_left_influence > 0.1 }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_left = 0.01 }
					set_variable = { mcs_left_satisfaction_change = -0.2 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { mcs_fascist_influence > 0.1 }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_fascist = 0.01 }
					set_variable = { mcs_fascist_satisfaction_change = -0.1 }
				}
				mcs_influence_calculation = yes
				mcs_unity_check = yes
			}
		}
	}
	mcs_talk_to_leaders_south = {
		icon = GFX_decision_USA_npp_n
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP
		}
		cost = 10
		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = MCS_talk_to_south
			hidden_effect = {
				subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_center = 0.015 }
				add_to_variable = { mcs_change_influence_right = 0.005 }
				add_to_variable = { mcs_change_influence_south = 0.01 }
				set_variable = { mcs_center_satisfaction_change = -0.2 }
				set_variable = { mcs_right_satisfaction_change = 0.05 }
				set_variable = { mcs_south_satisfaction_change = 0.1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { mcs_left_influence > 0.1 }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_left = 0.01 }
					set_variable = { mcs_left_satisfaction_change = -0.2 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { mcs_fascist_influence > 0.1 }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_fascist = 0.01 }
					set_variable = { mcs_fascist_satisfaction_change = 0.1 }
				}
				mcs_influence_calculation = yes
				mcs_unity_check = yes
			}
		}
	}
	mcs_publicly_support_center = {
		icon = GFX_decision_USA_npp_p
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP
		}
		cost = 25
		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = MCS_public_support_center
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							AND = {
								check_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity > NPP_FR_bonus_popularity }
								check_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity > RD_D_bonus_popularity }
							}
						}
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.01 }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.015 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.01 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.015 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								AND = {
									check_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity > NPP_FR_bonus_popularity }
									check_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity < RD_D_bonus_popularity }
								}
								AND = {
									check_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity < NPP_FR_bonus_popularity }
									check_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity > RD_D_bonus_popularity }
								}
							}
						}
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.005 }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.005 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.005 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.005 }
					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.01 }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.005 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.01 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.005 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
					}
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = progressivism

######### OFN Membership decisions

USA_OFN_membership_category = {
	OFN_open_negotiations_with = {
		visible = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = OFN_opposes_new_member
					has_country_flag = OFN_neutral_new_member
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = OFN_membership_costs_trigger
				OR = {
					check_variable = { political_power > FROM.OFN_convince_cost_political }
					check_variable = { money_reserves > FROM.OFN_convince_cost_money }
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = OFN_membership_negotiation_trigger
				NOT = { has_country_flag = OFN_currently_negotiating_with_someone }
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision OFN_open_negotiations_with target: [From.GetName]"
			custom_effect_tooltip = OFN_membership_start_negotiations
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { USA_currently_negotiating_with = FROM.id }
				set_variable = { USA_current_political_cost = FROM.OFN_convince_cost_political }
				set_variable = { USA_current_money_cost = FROM.OFN_convince_cost_money }
				set_country_flag = OFN_currently_negotiating_with_someone
				country_event = { id = OFN.membership.100 }
			}
		}
	}
	OFN_admit_member = {
		allowed = { tag = USA }
		visible = { has_country_flag = USA_OFN_new_membership_application }
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = OFN_membership_all_in_favor
				all_of_scopes = {
					array = global.OFN_members
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = OFN_supports_new_member
						is_subject = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		complete_effect = {
			USA = { add_to_faction = OFN_candidate }
			add_to_array = {
				global.OFN_members = var:OFN_candidate
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { OFN_candidate = IBR.id }
				}
				IBR = {
					add_ideas = OFN_Independent_Member
					country_event = {
						id = IBR.707
					}
				}
			}
			USA_OFN_clear_candidate_vote = yes
		}
	}
	OFN_addition_timeout = {
		allowed = { tag = USA }
		visible = { has_country_flag = USA_OFN_new_membership_application }
		available = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_OFN_new_membership_application } }
		activation = { has_country_flag = USA_OFN_new_membership_application }
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { OFN_candidate = IBR.id }
				}
				IBR = {
					country_event = {
						id = IBR.706
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_can_grant_iberia_observer_status
			}
			USA_OFN_clear_candidate_vote = yes
		}
		complete_effect = { }
	}
	OFN_grant_observer_status_iberia = {
		allowed = { tag = USA }
		visible = { has_country_flag = USA_can_grant_iberia_observer_status }
		complete_effect = {
			IBR = { country_event = { id = IBR.711 } }
			clr_country_flag = USA_can_grant_iberia_observer_status
		}
	}

	USA_NPP_Denounce_Japanese_Imperialism_Decision = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_propaganda

		visible = { has_completed_focus = USA_Community_Action }

		available = {
			has_country_flag = npp_fp_chose_revanchism
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_NPP_FP_already_doing_decision }
		}

		cost = npp_fp_rally_cost

		days_re_enable = 120

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_NPP_popularity_grows_low
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_government = paternalism }
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_L_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_Y_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_government = progressivism }
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_L_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_Y_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_government = national_socialism }
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_Y_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_L_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_government = communist }
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_L_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_Y_bonus_popularity = 0.008 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
